 samit patel 30 ran banaakar naabad laute

 iske baad captain elister cook (17) or petersan ne duusare wicket ke liye 54 ran jode lekin bhubaneshwar ne is jodi ko safal nahin hone diya
 Cook hit three fours off 27 balls

 Earlier, India won the toss and scored 285 for six wickets in the allotted 50 overs, batting first
 captain mahendra singh dhoni ne 72 ranon kii pari kheli jabaki rabindra jadeja ne naabad 61 ran banaae
 Apart from these two, Suresh Raina contributed 55 and Virat Kohli contributed 37 runs
 yuvaraj singh ne apni 32 ranon kii pari main paanch chauke lagaae
 Dhoni faced 66 balls and hit seven fours and two sixes in his innings
 unka wicket 270 ranon ke kul yoga par gira
 Dhoni and Jedja shared a 96-run partnership for the sixth wicket to bring India to a respectable score
 bharat kii pari shuruyaat acchhee nahin rahi
 Both his openers Gautam Gambhir and Ajinkya Rahane returned to the pavilion for a total of 18 runs
 bharat kaa pehla wicket gambheer ke rup main gira
 He was bowled by Jade Dernbach for a personal score of eight
 unke baad rahane bhi zyada der tak nahin tik sake or steven fin kii gend par clin bold ho gaye
 After this, Yuvraj and Kohli showed good batting and the team recovered from the initial shaking
 donon ke bich tisare wicket ke liye 53 ranon kii mahatvapurn saajhedaari hui
 In the 16th over, Yuvraj was trapped leg before by spinner James Tradwell
 bharat kaa chauthaa wicket kohli ke rup main gira
 He was caught by Ian Bell off Chris Woakes
 tippaniyan After the dismissals of Yuvraj and Kohli, the Indian innings looked once again faltering, but Raina played a decent innings, showing the wisdom
 raina or dhoni ke bich paanchaven wicket ke liye 55 ranon kii saajhedaari hui
 India's sixth wicket fell as Dhoni
 unhen dernbank kii gend par joe root ne seemaa rekha ke paas kaich kiya

 logon ko unhen sanyas lene kii salaah dena band karnaa chahie
 'we must applaud Sachin for everything he has done for the game
 kisi ko bhi unhen yah nahin poochna chahie ki aap kab sanyas le rahe hai

 ' Bihar Chief Minister and Janata Dal United (JDU) President Nitish Kumar once again wants Prime Minister Narendra Modi to form the government at the Center
 yun to sahyogi ke rup main nitish kumaar kii is chahat main koi kaami nahin he lekin wo apane bhaashan main iske kaaran ginate hai
 According to Nitish, the central government which has helped Bihar during Prime Minister Modi's time will continue continuously
 nitish ke anusaar agar centre main modi sarkaar rahegi tab hi bihar kaa pichhadaapan dur hoga or vikaas hoga
 Nitish mentions about 50 thousand crore projects approved by the Center, especially in the road sector, under which many state highways have now been converted into national highways and construction of several new bridges has been started
 nitish apane bhaashan main logon ke saamne pradhanmantri narendra modi kii tarifon ke pul baandhne main bhi koi kasar nahin chhodte
 Especially the work that has been done for the common people, for the poor, it is a matter of attention in the country
 garib parivaar kii mahilaon ko khaanaa banane main kitni pareshaani hoti thi, dhuaan jhelana padataa tha
 After that, under the Pradhan Mantri Ujjwala scheme, poor families started getting LPG connections free of cost
 iske baad garib parivaar ke logon ke liye ilaaj, ayushmaan bharat ke tahat paanch lakh rupaya kii yojana kii shuruyaat kar di gai
